Oh, sons, since I have completed this book for you, which is the end of medical science, and its completion has achieved its purpose in it, and through its explanations and declarations, it seems to me that you can comprehend this treatise, which is part of surgery with my hands.
Since surgery with my hands is practiced in our region and at our time, it has been hidden, except that its danger and sight are frightening; and there remain from it only some small descriptions in the books of the Ancients, which have changed much and led to those errors and hesitation, until their intentions are clear and its strength and art have been lost.
And it seems to me that you revive that ancient order of this treatise through its second way of exposition and declaration and abbreviation; and so I have added the forms of cauterizing instruments and other tools of the craft as an addition of explanation and preparation for them, which is necessary.
But the reason why a skilled craftsman with their own hands cannot be found in our time is because the art of medicine is long and requires its practitioner to have been exercised in the science of anatomy, which Galen knew well, as he understood the joints of the members and their forms, and the conjunction and separation of them; and knowledge of the bones, nerves, and ligaments, and their number, and the arrangement of them; and the pulsating and quiet veins, and the places of their outflow.
And because of this, Hippocrates said that in a name there is virtue, but more so in the work itself, and especially in the art of the hand.
Those who are not familiar with the anatomy that we have discussed in the beginning of this book will be at risk of falling into error, and thus may cause harm to men, as I have seen many such individuals, for some are trained in this science but do not practice it.
For you have seen a foolish doctor, full of pride, cause an abscess in the neck of a woman and cut into some arteries of her neck so that great blood flowed out while the woman died between his own hands.
And I have seen another doctor who was so confident that he would remove an arrow from a man who had been injured in his state, and the arrow was large, and came to him and with great haste removed this arrow along with a piece of the viscera, by which the man died on the third day.
And I have already cried out against him and seen that due to the size of the arrow and the condition of the patient, he knew beforehand that the man would die.
And I saw another surgeon who was being paid by a duke of our land for surgery, and he entrusted to a blacksmith the repair of a fracture in the patient's leg; and because the surgeon was ignorant, without taking out the fragments, with forceps and splints tightened strongly on the wound, and did not give the wound any air.
And he loosed the stitches according to their desires, and let the limb rest, and ordered that we loosen the bandage after some days, and commanded us to untie the binding; and it happened this way that the bone and the skin became suppurated, and came to corruption.
And I was called to him, and I prepared myself to loosen the binding, and succeeded in calming him down and alleviating his pain.
But however, the corruption was already confirmed in the member, so I couldn't stop it, and the corruption continued to spread in the member until the patient fell into a serious condition.
And I saw another surgeon who pierced a cancerous abscess, and it was ulcerated after several days, until the wickedness of him was magnified before his lord.
Which is because the cancerous sore is pure of melancholic humour, and therefore it does not need to be treated with iron tools, but rather is a member which suffers and should be healed. The cure of intestinal hernia.
The occurrence of this hernia is due to a section that becomes adherent on the navel extended over the abdomen from the wounds of the navel, so that descending the intestines through this rupture.
And this rupture is either of the navel or an exit from it, and accidents occur in these two species for many causes: or a blow, or a sudden effort, or shouting, or elevation due to some serious cause, or likeness.
And the sign of this, when it is due to extension of the navel, is that the accident happens little by little over a long time, and does not happen suddenly, and it becomes an abscess in front of the pubic bone because the navel compresses the intestine.
And the sign of this is when it is due to section of the navel, because at first it makes violent pain suddenly; and there are multiple abscesses visible below the skin that has been cut open, and this is due to the bursting of the intestine, and the body of it breaks through the parts outside of the navel.

And in the treatment of these types of illnesses with iron, there is fear of cutting or perforating something in that area.

And then you cut out the skin that covers the testicles, up to where the white, hard scrotal sac is revealed on each side.

And then you take the skin of the testicles with your hand and push it forward, and at the same time extend the white scrotal sac with your left hand, and lift up the wound to the part of the section; and command the assistant to stretch out the wound upwards and dissolve the adhesion that is behind with a completed solution.
And then look carefully at the parts you said were not to be any cause of the intestine being wrapped in the white, hard scrotal sac. But if you find any cause there, then immediately put it into the belly behind. (Note: "enpelleys" is an archaic or poetic way of saying "put in")
